data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.0">Portland Timbers 3, FC Dallas 1 | MLS Cup Playoffs Match Recap</h1><div class="byline" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1"><address class="author" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.0"><a data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.0.0" href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/author/Dan Itel" rel="author">Dan Itel</a></address><time class="pubdate" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.1.1" datetime="2015-11-23">Nov 23, 2015</time></div><div data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.2"></div><div data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.3" id="ooyala-player-BnZzUyeTpBEttzJuL6YIWXt1g1nDVn1O"></div><div class="gigya-share" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.4" id="article-share"></div><img class="article-primary-image" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.5" src="http://league-mp7static.mlsdigital.net/styles/image_default/s3/images/POR_DAL_FINAL-1.jpg"><article class="article" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.6"><p>PORTLAND, Ore.\xe2\x80\x94With an attack-oriented 3-1 victory over FC Dallas on Sunday at Providence Park, the Portland Timbers discarded any notion they would try to make a cagey affair out of the first leg of their Audi 2015 MLS Cup Playoffs Western Conference Championship.</p>\n<p>The Timbers used a first-half goal from <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/liam-ridgewell">Liam Ridgewell</a>, a stunning long-distance blast from <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/dairon-asprilla">Dairon Asprilla</a> just after halftime and a finisher from <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/nat-borchers">Nat Borchers</a> in stoppage time to leave the conference\xe2\x80\x99s No. 1 seed with a tough climb when the series resumes in a week\xe2\x80\x99s time at Toyota Stadium in Frisco, Texas.</p>\n<p>Facing a 2-0 deficit, Dallas staved off complete disaster with a 62nd-minute strike by <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/david-texeira">David Texeira</a>, a goal that could prove to be key should the series come down to the away-goal tiebreaker.</p>\n<p>Despite the absences of playmaker <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/diego-valeri">Diego Valeri</a> and winger <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/rodney-wallace">Rodney Wallace</a> due to yellow-card accumulation, the Timbers came out of the gates flying \xe2\x80\x93 nearly sneaking in the opener before the end of the opening minute.</p>\n<p>It all started with the first of many blistering counters led by attacking midfielder <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/darlington-nagbe">Darlington Nagbe</a>, who assumed Valeri\xe2\x80\x99s normal role. Nagbe played through to <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/lucas-melano">Lucas Melano</a> on the right wing for a shot on goal 30 seconds after the opening whistle that had to be turned away by Dallas goalkeeper <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/jesse-gonzalez">Jesse Gonzalez</a>.</p>\n<p>In the fourth minute, Portland were at it once again off Nagbe&amp;apos;s playmaking: he (again) pushed wide to Melano, whose chip shot across the goalmouth was spilled by Gonzalez before a clearance.</p>\n<p>In the 21st minute, Texeira pinged a restart into the box back out to <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/mauro-diaz">Mauro Diaz</a> for a shot on target that was easily dealt with by Timbers \xe2\x80\x98keeper <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/adam-kwarasey">Adam Kwarasey</a>.</p>\n<p>Portland\xe2\x80\x99s opener came two minutes later, when Nagbe\xe2\x80\x99s corner was flicked on by a Asprilla header; Ridgewell bundled it across the line.</p>\n<p>The Timbers threatened nearly adding their second in the 47th minute, when Asprilla redirected a corner kick to the top shelf, where it was palmed over by Gonzalez.</p>\n<p>But Asprilla wouldn\xe2\x80\x99t be denied: In the 53rd minute, he took a touch into space before unleashing a right-footed 30-yard blast past Gonzalez and into the far, top corner.</p>\n<p>Dallas finally began to respond in the 55th minute; Michael Barrios peeled off a contested shot in the box that flew just high. Two minutes later, Diaz played through <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/ryan-hollingshead">Ryan Hollingshead</a> for a 1-on-1 with Kwarasey \xe2\x80\x93 who was caught off his line \xe2\x80\x93 but Hollingshead&amp;apos;s shot was directed into the side netting.</p>\n<p>They broke through shortly after, when Texeira tapped home a simple cross from <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/je-vaughn-watson">Je-Vaughn Watson</a> from the right flank for the crucial away goal.</p>\n<p>The Timbers regained their two-goal advantage off a corner kick one minute into stoppage time; Borchers cleaned up an initial header from second-half substitute <a href="http://www.mlssoccer.com/players/norberto-paparatto">Norberto Paparatto</a> to leave the sell-out crowd (21,144)\xc2\xa0in euphoria after their final home game of 2015.</p>\n</article><div class="gigya-comments" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.0.0.8" id="article-comments"></div></img></div></div><div class="ad-wrapper" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.9.1.0.3.$recap.1.1" id="matchcenter-recap-1"></div></div></div></section></div></section></main><div class="connection-warning" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.a" style="pointer-events:none;">Connection Lost. Reconnecting...</div><div class="back-to-top nodelay" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.b"><i class="fa fa-arrow-up" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.b.0"></i></div><div class="stat-share-overlay" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.c"><div class="stat-share-modal" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.c.0"><h2 data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.c.0.0"><span data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.c.0.0.0"></span><i class="fa fa-times close-modal" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.c.0.0.1"></i></h2><div class="preview" data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.c.0.2"><p data-reactid=".18y5ktxwjk0.c.0.2.3">Generate a preview before
